    &lt;div data-bind="visible: showWeekly"&gt;&lt;br/&gt;Rightmove has calculated the price per MONTH for comparison purposes only.
        &lt;br/&gt;The method we use for calculating the monthly price is: (weekly price x 52) / 12, rounded to the nearest pound. We provide the monthly price for comparison purposes only; agents may calculate a monthly price in different ways.
        &lt;br/&gt;Please check with &lt;span data-bind="text: marketedBy"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;  for details.
    &lt;/div&gt;
    &lt;div data-bind="visible: showMonthly"&gt;&lt;br/&gt;Rightmove has calculated the price per WEEK for comparison purposes only.
        &lt;br/&gt;The method we use for calculating the weekly price is: (monthly price x 12) / 52, rounded to the nearest pound. We provide the monthly price for comparison purposes only; agents may calculate a monthly price in different ways.
        &lt;br/&gt;Please check with &lt;span data-bind="text: marketedBy"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;  for details.
    &lt;/div&gt;

    &lt;div data-bind="visible: showQuarterly"&gt;&lt;br/&gt;Rightmove has calculated the price per MONTH and the price per WEEK to make comparison with other properties in the area easier.
        &lt;br/&gt;The method we use for calculating the monthly price is: (quarterly price x 4) / 12, rounded to the nearest pound. We provide the monthly price for comparison purposes only; agents may calculate a monthly price in different ways.
        &lt;br/&gt;Please check with &lt;span data-bind="text: marketedBy"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;  for details.
        &lt;br/&gt;The method we use for calculating the weekly price is: (quarterly price x 4) / 52, rounded to the nearest pound. We provide the weekly price for comparison purposes only; agents may calculate a weekly price in different ways.
        &lt;br/&gt;Please check with &lt;span data-bind="text: marketedBy"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;  for details.
    &lt;/div&gt;

        &lt;br/&gt;The method we use for calculating the monthly price is: (yearly price x 1) / 12, rounded to the nearest pound. We provide the monthly price for comparison purposes only; agents may calculate a monthly price in different ways.
        &lt;br/&gt;The method we use for calculating the weekly price is: (yearly price x 1) / 52, rounded to the nearest pound. We provide the weekly price for comparison purposes only; agents may calculate a weekly price in different ways.
        &lt;br/&gt;Please check with &lt;span data-bind="text: marketedBy"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;  for details.
